Important Items List

Currently, only a portion of items useful for higher playthroughs has been organized. More content is being added, but due to limited energy, please be patient...

Somber Ancient Dragon Smithing Stone

  • 1. (Ranni the Witch's Side Quest) Reward for completing Latenna's questline
  • 2. (Millicent's Side Quest) If you choose to assist during Millicent's questline, you can obtain it after defeating ü¶ÅMalenia, by interacting with the flower left in the boss room with the Golden Needle.
  • 3. Along the path from the grace point of the Mongwyn Dynasty Dynasty Mausoleum Midpoint, it can be obtained from a chest in front of a statue after seeing an enemy.
  • 4. From the body near the ancient dragon close to the crumbling grace point of Faram Azula Dragon Church (Rooftop).
  • 5. Can be obtained from a body on the right side of the bridge next to the grace point "Erdtree Branch" Ebreitas Prayer Room.
  • 6. Can also be obtained from the chest above the location of the dung beetle, to the left of the grace point "Erdtree Branch" Ebreitas Prayer Room, by crossing the railing.
  • 7. Can be picked up from a body near the castle of Greyoll's Dragonbarrow.
  • 8. In the western part of the grace point Consecrated Snowfield (Depths), obtained by defeating the invader Anastasia.

Ancient Dragon Smithing Stone

  • 1. By giving 9 Deathroots (methods of obtaining are listed on this page) to the NPC üê©Beast Clergyman Gurranq at the grace point north of Gelmir, you can obtain it (or by killing him directly).
  • 2. (Sorceress Sellen's Side Quest) At the end of the questline, do not choose to help üßôSellen, but kill her instead (hostile route). You can obtain it after defeating Sellen and talking to Jerren.
  • 3. On a body inside a giant skull to the southeast of the grace point at the Giant's Summit Church of Rest.
  • 4. On a body inside the Yelough Anix Tunnel to the southwest of the Giant's Summit west side Consecrated Snowfield.
  • 5. Near the body close to the "Great Earth Dragon" Seethewaterik at the grace point inside the Giant's Summit west side Cave of Solace.
  • 6. By heading southwest from the grace point at the Giant's Summit west side Consecrated Snowfield (Depths) and defeating ü¶ÅNight's Cavalry (Bladed Halberd) and ü¶ÅNight's Cavalry (Flail), you can obtain it.
  • 7. By defeating the ancient dragon in front of the crumbling grace point of Faram Azula Gradually Collapsing Beast Grave.
  • 8. At the grace point Dragon Church (Rooftop), by defeating the ancient dragon ahead, you can obtain it.
  • 9. At the grace point Dragon Church Altar, by going around to the rooftop and jumping to the left platform, you can obtain it.
  • 10. In front of the grace point of Miquella's Haligtree Haligtree Town, in front of the lion hybrid, you can obtain it.
  • 11. Near the ladder by Miquella's Haligtree grace point Haligtree Promenade, by climbing down and then going up the stairs from outside, opening the chest in front can obtain it.
  • 12. (Nepheli Loux's Side Quest) Obtain by talking to Nepheli Loux after completing her questline.
  • 13. (Nepheli Loux's Side Quest) Obtain by purchasing from the shop of Gatekeeper Gostoc after completing her questline.

Great Grave Glovewort

  • 1. From the grace point of the Consecrated Snowfield (Depths), head southeast to the dungeon Consecrated Snowfield Catacombs, defeat ü¶ÅCorrupted Gravekeeper to obtain it.
  • 2. Northwest of the grace point Church of Rest, in the hero's graveyard of the Giant War, obtained behind a Flame Monk.
  • 3. In the gradually collapsing region of Faram Azula, from the grace point Beast Grave (Depths), obtained in front of a creature.
  • 4. In the gradually collapsing region of Faram Azula, from the grace point Dragon Church, jump down, climb up the stairs, and obtain it inside a room.
  • 5. From the grace point of Miquella's Haligtree Drainage Channel, go back, cross the branches, and obtain it at the deepest part of the mud pond (beware of the hidden BOSS in the mud pond).

Great Ghost Glovewort

  • 1. In Ainsel River, can be obtained from a chest in the room below the giant skeleton statue after defeating the boss.
  • 2. Forward from the grace point Night's Sacred Ground, obtained from a chest under the giant skeleton statue.
  • 3. From the grace point Eternal City, go straight, cross the bridge, and it's found in a chest behind a narrow room (beware of Silver Tear mimicking a giant iron ball hanging from the ceiling).
  • 4. Obtained in a room at the grace point Spiritcaller's Dynasty (Midsection).
  • 5. Supposed to be in the Spiritcaller's Dynasty, not yet discovered.

Ritual Pot

  • 1. North of the grace point Raya Lucaria Ruins by Lake Liurnia.
  • 2. At the end of the main path inside the grace point Schoolhouse Classroom.
  • 3. Near Pot Village by Lake Liurnia (1).
  • 4. Near Pot Village by Lake Liurnia (2).
  • 5. Purchased from a merchant at the hermit's broken house to the left of the Dragonbarrow.
  • 6. Purchased from Servant Biddy at Fort Gael.
  • 7. Picked up inside the catacombs of the Altus Plateau Subterranean Shunning-Grounds (1).
  • 8. Picked up inside the catacombs of the Altus Plateau Subterranean Shunning-Grounds (2).
  • 9. At the elevator entrance before Abandoned Cave of Omen.
  • 10. In a room in the Giant's Summit Catacombs in the southern snowfield.

Deathroot

  • 1. Obtained by defeating Tibia's Summoning Boat in Summonwater Village.
  • 2. Obtained from a chest after defeating a boss in Catacombs of the Death-Bringer.
  • 3. Obtained by defeating Tibia's Summoning Boat near the Caria Manor.
  • 4. Obtained from a chest after defeating a boss in Black Knife Catacombs.
  • 5. Obtained from a chest after defeating a boss in Gelmir Hero's Grave.
  • 6. Obtained by defeating Tibia's Summoning Boat near the ruins by the hill close to the Erdtree.
  • 7. West of the grace point Frozen Lake, obtained by defeating Tibia's Summoning Boat.
  • 8. Obtained from a chest after defeating a boss in Giant's Summit Catacombs.
  • 9. Obtained from a chest after defeating a boss through an invisible path towards the Secret Path to the Haligtree.

Full Storyline Walkthrough

DLC content has not been added yet
The place names in the walkthrough only represent progress and do not strictly indicate where the storyline events occur.

Chapel of Anticipation Chapel of Anticipation

  • Obtain the gesture "Ring of the Erdtree" at birth, item Tarnished's Wizened Finger is by the dead witch's right hand.
  • Defeat ü¶Å"Grafted" Scion, obtain the item Cerulean Amber Medallion, or trigger the storyline by dying.

Limgrave Limgrave

  • Jump down to the right for the grace point Cave of Knowledge. Defeat Soldier of Godrick along the way to pick up the gesture "Furl Calling Finger Remedy" by the cliff.
  • After taking the elevator, there's a grace point First Step outside.
  • (White Mask Side Quest) Talk to White Mask Varr√© in front of the grace point.
  • Pass by Tree Sentinel to reach grace point Church of Elleh, trigger dialogue with Merchant Kale.
  • Continue northeast to rest at grace point Gatefront, triggering Melina's storyline and obtaining the Spectral Steed Whistle.
  • Return to grace point Church of Elleh, rest until night to trigger Ranni's story.
  • Return to grace point Gatefront, head south to get the map by the stone, obtain the Whetstone Knife in the dungeon nearby.
  • (Tailor Patches Side Quest) Continue south to the forest near the telescope to find Tailor Patches and trigger dialogue.
  • (Sorceress Sellen Side Quest) Cross the bridge to the south, in the Waypoint Ruins dungeon, defeat ü¶ÅMad Pumpkin Head, find Sorceress Sellen, trigger dialogue, and obtain the gesture "Nod in Agreement".
  • (Roderika Side Quest) Return to grace point Gatefront and head north to reach grace point Stormhill Shack, rest at grace to trigger dialogue with Melina. Then talk to Roderika inside the shack.
  • (Knight Bernahl Side Quest) From grace point Stormhill Shack head east to grace point Warmaster's Shack, rest at grace to trigger dialogue with Melina, then talk to Knight Bernahl inside the shack.
  • (‚ÄúJar Warrior‚Äù Alexander Side Quest) Continue east to grace point Saintsbridge nearby, head towards the shouting from the south, find ‚ÄúJar Warrior‚Äù Alexander to trigger dialogue.
  • (‚ÄúD‚Äù Side Quest) From grace point Saintsbridge head east across the bridge, find D by the roadside to trigger dialogue.
  • (‚ÄúD‚Äù Side Quest) Continue east past grace point Outside Summonwater Village to Summonwater Village, defeat ü¶ÅTibia's Summoning Boat, find D right beside the village to trigger dialogue.
  • Head south to grace point Third Church of Marika to rest, triggering dialogue with Melina.
  • (Hyetta Side Quest) From grace point Third Church of Marika head west, trigger dialogue with ‚ÄúLord's Firstborn‚Äù Kenneth Haight on the bridge.
  • (Blaise the Half-Wolf Side Quest) Continue south, past the Mistwood Ruins, after hearing the wolf howl, teleport back to Church of Elleh, trigger dialogue with Merchant Kale to obtain the Snap gesture. Then return to Mistwood Ruins, use the gesture, and talk to Blaise the Half-Wolf.
  • Head south into Fort Haight, where you can obtain the item Dectus Medallion (Left).
  • (Hyetta Side Quest) After clearing Fort Haight, return to the bridge and talk with Kenneth Haight. Return to Fort Haight again, talk with Kenneth Haight on the wall above.
  • (Blaise the Half-Wolf Side Quest) From grace point South of Lake of Rot head south to "Masterless Hound's Prison", enter and summon Blaise the Half-Wolf, talk with him after defeating the boss. Teleport back to Church of Elleh and talk with Merchant Kale.
  • (Yura Side Quest) By grace point Seaside Ruins, you can talk with ‚ÄúBloody Finger‚Äù Yura.
  • (Yura Side Quest) From grace point Seaside Ruins head north, through the lake area to encounter boss üê≤‚ÄúFlying Dragon‚Äù Agheel, defeat it, return to Yura for new dialogue.
  • (Yura Side Quest) Continue north, encounter ‚ÄúBloody Finger‚Äù Nerijus red phantom invasion before the ‚ÄúMourne Tunnel‚Äù entrance, wait a moment for ‚ÄúBloody Finger Hunter‚Äù Yura to come help
  • (Yura Side Quest) After defeating ‚ÄúBloody Finger‚Äù Nerijus, you can find Yura for dialogue below the northern cliff.
  • (Patches Side Quest) Enter Mourne Tunnel, bring ü¶ÅPatches down to half health, accept his plea for mercy (attacking him once more after the plea grants an emote). Refresh the area at a grace point, then return to Patches for dialogue. Open the nearby chest to trigger a cutscene.
  • (Tailor Patches Side Quest) From the grace point First Step head west, find Tailor near the grace point Coastal Cave for dialogue. You can summon ‚ÄúAncient Knight‚Äù Istvan to defeat the boss and obtain the Sewing Needle, then talk to Tailor again.

Weeping Peninsula Weeping Peninsula

  • (Irina of Mourn's Side Quest) South of the grace point Bridge of Sacrifice, talk to Irina of Mourn, then head south to Fort Mourn, defeat ü¶ÅLion Guardian, and talk to Lord Edgar.
  • (Irina of Mourn's Side Quest) Return to grace point Bridge of Sacrifice and talk to Irina of Mourn and Lord Edgar nearby.
  • Rest at grace point Pilgrimage Church to trigger dialogue with Melina
  • Yet to be discovered

Stormveil Castle Stormveil Castle

  • From the grace point Stormhill Shack head north, enter the castle gate, pass through the grace point Rampart Tower, defeat Boss ‚ÄúGodrick the Grafted‚Äù, triggering the Roundtable Hold storyline.
  • (Diallos Side Quest) Talk to Diallos at the Roundtable Hold
  • (Gideon Side Quest) Talk to Gideon at the Roundtable Hold
  • (‚ÄúD‚Äù Side Quest) Talk to ‚ÄúD‚Äù at the Roundtable Hold
  • (Colin Side Quest) Talk to Colin at the Roundtable Hold
  • (Gatekeeper Gostoc Side Quest) Along the way, talk to Gatekeeper Gostoc in a small hut near grace point Stormveil Main Gate.
  • (Gatekeeper Gostoc Side Quest) Proceed along the small path to explore to a small hut by the grace point, then head up into the tower, exit the tower, return the same way, on the small slope beside grace point Stormveil Cliffside to find Gostoc for dialogue
  • (Gatekeeper Gostoc Side Quest) In a room near the entrance, entering will get you locked inside by Gostoc
  • (Roderika Side Quest) Find the item ‚ÄúRemembrance of the Grafted‚Äù in the castle, then go to grace point Stormhill Shack, talk to Roderika inside the shack.
  • (Roderika Side Quest) Return to the Roundtable Hold to talk with Roderika, then alternate between talking to the blacksmith Hewg and Roderika. Refresh the map and talk to them again.
  • (Sorcerer Rogier Side Quest) In the northwest part of the castle by the altar, you can find Sorcerer Rogier, triggering dialogue.
  • (Nepheli Loux Side Quest) Inside a house in front of the grace point Small Room Deep Within, you can find Warrior Nepheli Loux, triggering dialogue with her
  • (Sorcerer Rogier Side Quest) At the bottom of the castle, after defeating Putrid Tree Spirit, you can find Sorcerer Rogier's bloodstain in the boss arena.
  • Return to Small Room Deep Within, in front of the boss door you can summon Nepheli Loux, defeat üßü‚ÄúGrafted‚Äù Godrick. After resting at grace, you can see Gatekeeper Gostoc.
  • (Sorcerer Rogier Side Quest) After defeating üßü‚ÄúGrafted‚Äù Godrick, Sorcerer Rogier will return to the Roundtable Hold, triggering dialogue.
  • (Nepheli Loux Side Quest) After defeating üßü‚ÄúGrafted‚Äù Godrick, Nepheli Loux will return to the Roundtable Hold, talk to her to obtain items, then you can talk to Gideon.
  • (Witch Renna Side Quest) In the room after defeating üßü‚ÄúGrafted‚Äù Godrick, find the item ‚ÄúGrapes‚Äù.
  • (Witch Renna Side Quest) By grace point Lakeside Cliff, you can meet Witch Renna, give her ‚ÄúGrapes‚Äù. This side quest requires completion of the Irina of Mourn side quest beforehand.
  • (Tailor Patches Side Quest) At the grace point Lakeside Cliff, you can talk to Patches, then rest at the grace to have a dialogue with Melina (If Patches is not at this grace, try passing time to night or after reaching the grace point Raya Lucaria Gate to talk again)
  • (White Mask Side Quest) Return to grace point First Step to see a message from White Mask Varr√©.

Liurnia Liurnia

  • (Sorcerer Thops Side Quest) From Lakeside Cliff, talk to Sorcerer Thops at the Church of Irith.
  • (Rya Side Quest) In front of grace point Raya Lucaria Ruins, near the telescope, you can talk to ‚ÄúRecusant‚Äù Rya to accept a quest, triggering the Volcano Manor storyline. (One way to enter Volcano Manor)
  • (Patches Side Quest) A short distance forward, at grace point Island of Farum Azula, you can talk to Patches.
  • (Rya Side Quest) At Boiled Prawn Shack grace point, talk to the NPC Bandit nearby, choose to buy to get Rya's Necklace, return it to Rya.
  • (Dung Eater Side Quest) Talk to the Bandit again, choose to buy prawns, talk.
  • (Diallos Side Quest) Arrive at grace point Academy Gate Town, you can find Diallos to the north, trigger dialogue. Then return to the Roundtable Hold for another dialogue.
  • (Witch Renna Side Quest) At grace point Raya Lucaria Ruins on the east side, find purified ruins to get Grapes. Give them to Witch Renna nearby.
  • (Irina of Mourn's Side Quest) At grace point Avenger's Shack, trigger Lord Edgar's invasion, defeat him to get Grapes. Irina of Mourn's side quest concludes here.
  • (Witch Renna Side Quest) At grace point Town Gate Bridge, talk to Renna to the north, give her Grapes (perhaps her father's eyeball?). After refreshing the map, you can talk again.
  • At grace point Church Quarter north, you can find the Academy Glintstone Key, go to grace point Raya Lucaria (South Gate), touch the seal to enter the Academy.
  • (Yura Side Quest) From grace point Academy Main Gate, head north ignoring the seal for a while, you can find a red summon sign, help Yura defeat the boss, then talk to Yura.
  • (Sorcerer Thops Side Quest) Find the Academy Glintstone Key in the Academy. Return to the Church of Irith, talk to Thops.
  • (Sorcerer Thops Side Quest) From grace point Schoolhouse Classroom, head out the back door, you can find Thops. Return to the Church of Irith, defeat the Glintstone Dragon. Sorcerer Thops Side Quest concludes here.
  • (Tailor Patches Side Quest) Near grace point Church of Vows, pick up the item Golden Sewing Needle.
  • (Witch Renna Side Quest) At Bellum Church, talk to Renna.
  • (Witch Renna Side Quest) Near the Tranquil Church east of Bellum Church, defeat the invading Vicar, get a Finger Grape, return to Bellum Church and talk to Renna, handing over the Finger Grape.
  • (Pot Boy Side Quest) Arrive at the study's south side in Pot Village. Talk to Pot Boy. After refreshing the map, talk to Pot Boy again. Refresh the map once more and talk to Pot Boy. Keep refreshing the map and talking to Pot Boy. Continue this process.
  • (White Mask Side Quest) Come to the west side of the Academy Gate Town at the Rose Church, and talk to White Mask Varr√©, choose the suspicious option to receive the Festering Finger.
  • (White Mask Side Quest) Complete online invasions three times, find White Mask Varr√© to receive the item Tarnished's Oath Cloth.
  • (Nepheli Loux Side Quest) From the grace point next to the Four Belfries, open the chest to pick up the Magic Sword Key, head down towards the first tower, open the teleporter to be transported to the Prince of Death's Church, come to the rooftop via the small path, find the item Stormhawk King. Return to the Roundtable Hold and talk to Nepheli Loux.
  • (White Mask Side Quest) Interact with the deceased witch at the Prince of Death's Church, use the Oath Cloth to soak up the witch's blood
  • (Nepheli Loux Side Quest) Encounter Nepheli Loux at the entrance of the Platinum Village, triggering a dialogue. Afterwards, you can get help from Nepheli Loux in the Platinum Village Yellow Sign, defeating the Platinum Village Boss Omen Hunter.
  • (Sons of Platinum Side Quest) At the end of Platinum Village, find the disguised Albus, and talk to him to receive the item "Secret Medallion (Right)".
  • (Sons of Platinum Side Quest) Return to the Roundtable Hold, which will trigger the invasion plot of "Corpse-God" Niall. After defeating him, talk to Gideon Ofnir, and you can pick up Niall's equipment set at the entrance.
  • (Nepheli Loux Side Quest) Return to the Roundtable Hold and talk to Nepheli below the blacksmith, then find your foster father "Sir Gideon" to talk, and then talk to Nepheli again.
  • (Sons of Platinum Side Quest) Come to the south side of Liurnia near the Lakeside Crystal Cave. After defeating the boss Hound Knight, talk to Son of Platinum Letina nearby.
  • At the grace point Decaying Lift of Dectus, you can trigger a dialogue with Melina.
  • (Sorcerer Rogier Side Quest) Return to the Roundtable Hold and talk to Deathbed Companion Fia to receive a clue about the Black Knifeprint. From the grace point on the east side of Liurnia Ruins Labyrinth heading north, come to Black Knife Catacombs to receive the Black Knifeprint. Then talk to Rogier at the Roundtable Hold again.
  • (Sorcerer Rogier Side Quest) Talk to Deathbed Companion Fia again to inquire about Rogier. After refreshing the map, talk to Rogier to receive the Black Knifeprint and receive a clue about Ranni.
  • (Sorcerer Rogier Side Quest, Ranni Side Quest) From the grace point Road to the Manor heading north, after defeating the Caria Manor boss, you can come to Ranni's Magic Tower and talk to Witch Ranni. Then return to the Roundtable Hold and talk to Rogier.
  • (Witch Ranni Side Quest) Come to Ranni's Magic Tower again and talk to Witch Ranni. After talking to three people downstairs, return and talk to Ranni again.
  • (Sorcerer Seluvis Side Quest) Come to Sorcerer Seluvis's Tower and talk to Sorcery Teacher Seluvis to receive the item "Seluvis's Potion", do not use it yet.
  • (Sorcerer Seluvis Side Quest) From Ranni's Magic Tower heading east, you can jump from the cliff to the rooftop, go down through a hole in the roof, and talk to Servant Bid.
  • From the grace point Debate Parlor, take the right path, ride the elevator, enter the Grand Library, defeat "Full Moon Queen" Rennala.
  • (Gideon Side Quest) Return to the Roundtable Hold and talk to Gideon.

Siofra River Siofra River

  • From the grace point Marika's Third Church heading south, come to the entrance well of the Siofra River. Enter the underground world.
  • (Witch Ranni Side Quest) Near the grace point Siofra River (Shore), find "Half-Wolf" Blaidd, triggering dialogue.
  • (Sorcerer Seluvis Side Quest) Return to Sorcerer Seluvis's Tower and talk to Sorcery Teacher Seluvis to obtain Seluvis's Letter of Introduction.
  • (Sorcerer Seluvis Side Quest) In the Waystation Ruins Dungeon, find the sorcery teacher Sellen, triggering dialogue.
  • Return to the grace point Siofra River (Shore), and talk to "Half-Wolf" Blaidd.
  • (Alexander the Iron Fist Side Quest) In the middle of Siofra River, past the scaffolding, buy the item Warrior's Craft Notes 17 from the Abandoned Merchant, make the Oil Pot item.

Caelid Caelid

  • (Alexander the Iron Fist Side Quest) From the grace point Nokron, Eternal City, head east to reach Gael Tunnel. Find "Iron Fist" Alexander to trigger a dialogue.
  • (Millicent Side Quest) Go through Gael Tunnel, along the way until you reach the magic town of Sellia, talk to Sage Gowry at the entrance of the broken house.
  • (Millicent Side Quest) Head east to the center of Aeonian Swamp and defeat General Radahn to obtain the item Pure Gold Needle, return it to Sage Gowry, refresh the map, then find Gowry for a conversation again.
  • (Millicent Side Quest) Give the Golden Needle to Millicent at the Church of Inhibition, rest at the grace point, then you can talk again.
  • (Millicent Side Quest) After resting again, Millicent will leave, you can find her at Sage Gowry's place in the entrance of the broken house, triggering a conversation. Rest again to talk with Sage Gowry.
  • ("D" Side Quest) From the grace point Marika's Third Church, through the eastern teleporter, come to Caelid Bestial Sanctum, talk to "Beast Clergyman" Gurranq. Return to the grace point and talk to "D".
  • Come to the eastern part of Caelid, Fort Faroth, where you can obtain the Dectus Medallion (Right).
  • Come to the southeast of Caelid, the Redmane Castle, you can talk to multiple NPCs at Redmane Castle (Plaza) (including Witch-Hunter Jerren, "Half-Wolf" Blaidd, "Iron Fist" Alexander Side Quest), and finally defeat "Starscourge" Radahn.
  • (Half-Wolf Blaidd Side Quest) After defeating "Starscourge" Radahn, in the boss arena, you can find "Half-Wolf" Blaidd to trigger a dialogue.
  • ("Iron Fist" Alexander Side Quest) After defeating "Starscourge" Radahn, in the boss arena, you can find "Iron Fist" Alexander to trigger a dialogue.
  • ("Iron Fist" Alexander Side Quest) Return to the grace point Liurnia North Road, come to the south of Caria Manor, you can find "Iron Fist" Alexander, use the Oil Pot item, a strong attack can free him for a dialogue.
  • (Sorcery Teacher Sellen Side Quest) After defeating "Starscourge" Radahn, return to the grace point Waypoint Ruins, talk to Sellen (if you cannot trigger, please skip and complete the "Origin Mage" Azur quest in Altus Plateau before coming back).
  • (Sorcery Teacher Sellen Side Quest) Go to the ruins dungeon where the Witch is sealed, obtain Sellen's Primal Glintstone.
  • (Sorcery Teacher Sellen Side Quest) Return to Redmane Castle (Plaza) and talk to "Witch-Hunter" Jerren.
  • (Sorcery Teacher Sellen Side Quest) Return to the ruins dungeon where the Witch is sealed, and talk to "Witch-Hunter" Jerren.

Altus Plateau

  • Starting from the Grace Point East Gate of Stack Bridge in Liurnia, head north to reach Valley Bottom Village. At the entrance of the Lava Earth Dragon boss, you can summon "Great Horn" Tragoth, Millicent, Rogue.
  • Rest at the Altus Plateau Grace Point Near the Golden Tree Hill to trigger a conversation with Melina.
  • (Millicent Side Quest) Near the Altus Plateau Grace Point Near the Golden Tree Hill, you can find Millicent and talk to her.
  • (Rya Side Quest) Near the Altus Plateau Grace Point Near the Golden Tree Hill, you can find "Recruiter" Rya. You can choose to teleport to Volcano Manor, but it is recommended not to teleport.
  • (Dung Eater Side Quest) After lighting the first Grace in Altus Plateau, return to the Roundtable Hold and talk to Roderika to learn that the Dung Eater has returned to the Great Grace. Go and talk to him.
  • (Fia Side Quest) After lighting the first Grace in Altus Plateau, return to the Roundtable Hold and talk to Fia to receive the item "Invasion Short Sword."
  • (D Side Quest) Talk to D and give him the "Invasion Short Sword." Refresh the map and find D's items in the room near the blacksmith.
  • (Patches Side Quest) Head northwest and pass by the Grace Point Gelmir Volcano (First Rest Stop) on a cliff where you can see rainbow stones. Follow the rainbow stones to the edge of the cliff to trigger Patches' event.
  • (Alexander Side Quest) Walk counterclockwise from the valley to the west and reach the area near the Lava Earth Dragon to find "Great Jar Warrior" Alexander and trigger a conversation.
  • (Boc Side Quest) Continue walking counterclockwise and near the Secluded Village, pick up the item "You Look Good" from the mud skull.
  • (Sellen Side Quest) Continue walking counterclockwise and reach the area near "Origin Sorcerer" Azur. Talk to him to receive the spell Comet Azur. Return to the Grace Point Ruins of the Station Street and talk to Sellen to receive the Selia Seal Key.
  • (Volcano Manor Side Quest) From the Grace Point Road of Iniquity, head south to enter Volcano Manor. Talk to Tanith and join to receive the item "Guest Hall Key."
  • (Rya Side Quest) In the leftmost guest room inside Volcano Manor, you can talk to Rya.
  • (Diallos Side Quest) In the leftmost guest room inside Volcano Manor, you can talk to Diallos.
  • (Bernahl Side Quest) In the leftmost guest room inside Volcano Manor, you can talk to Knight Bernahl.
  • (Volcano Manor Side Quest) In the leftmost guest room inside Volcano Manor, pick up the item "Letter from Volcano Manor." Go to the Grace Point Warrior's Shack north of the marked point, defeat the red phantom NPC, and return to Volcano Manor to talk to Tanith. Enter the room again to pick up the item "Letter from Volcano Manor."
  • (Patches Side Quest) At the entrance of Volcano Manor, you can find Patches and trigger a conversation. Go to the Grace Point Lava Earth Dragon, defeat the red phantom NPC, and return to Volcano Manor to talk to Patches. Refresh the map to talk again.
  • (Volcano Manor Side Quest) Go to the room opposite the guest room and talk to the snake person. Then talk to Tanith.
  • (Volcano Manor Side Quest) From the Grace Point Near the Golden Tree Hill, head north to the marked point, defeat the red phantom NPC, and return to Volcano Manor to talk to Tanith.
  • (Bernahl Side Quest) You can talk to Knight Bernahl again in Volcano Manor.
  • (Diallos Side Quest) You can talk to Diallos again in Volcano Manor.
  • (Jar Side Quest) Go to Jarburg south of the Study Hall. Talk to the jar and Diallos. Refresh the map, talk to the jar and Diallos again. Refresh the map again to pick up equipment, then talk to the jar. Refresh the map once more and talk to the jar again.
  • (Rya Side Quest) After defeating the boss Godskin Noble in Volcano Manor, obtain the item "Serpent's Amnion." Return to Volcano Manor and talk to Rya. Talk to Tanith again to receive the item "Forgetfulness Potion."
  • (Millicent Side Quest) In a tower room in the city of Shade, obtain the item "Valkyrie's Prosthesis" from a chest. Return to the Grace Point Near the Golden Tree Hill and talk to Millicent. Then you can go to Caelid and talk to Sage Gowry.
  • (Goldmask Side Quest) Return to the Roundtable Hold and talk to Cleric Corhyn.
  • (Goldmask Side Quest) From the Grace Point Altus Highway Junction, head north to find Cleric Corhyn by the roadside and talk to him. Continue north, pass through the Forest-Spanning Greatbridge portal, find and talk to Goldmask, then return to Cleric Corhyn to talk again. Pass through the Forest-Spanning Greatbridge portal again, return to Goldmask and talk to Recorder Corhyn.
  • (Millicent Side Quest) At the Grace Point Windmill Village Heights in Windmill Village, you can summon Millicent. After defeating the Godskin boss, talk to Millicent.
  • (Yura Side Quest) Visit the Second Marika Cathedral and talk to Yura lying on the ground.
  • (Sellen Side Quest) Go to the hidden cave in Caelid Selia and talk to Luseth.
  • (Sellen Side Quest) Visit the underground chamber in Liurnia Selvis and interact with Sellen's body to transplant Sellen's Source Light Stone.
  • ÔºàSellen Side QuestÔºâReturn to the Grace Point Library of Raelucalia and speak with Sellen. Refresh the map and talk to the transformed Sellen.
  • ÔºàSellen Side QuestÔºâRefresh again, and two summoning symbols will appear at the door, leading you into a branching storyline. Branch One: Assist Sellen in defeating "Witch Hunter" Jelen. Obtain the Strange Knight Set. Branch Two: Aid Jelen in defeating Sellen. Acquire Sellen's Bell, Ancient Dragonstone. Conclusion of Sellen's storyline.
